<script>
var count = 1;
var Order = [];
var receipt_score = '0,0,0,0'.split(',');
var receipt_order = '1,2,3,4'.split(',');
var Score = [];
if(0 > 0){
  $('.contrl').hide();
}
$('.select').on('click', function(){
  var obj = event.target;
  obj.disabled = true;
  var st = 'img_id_'+obj.id.toString();
  $('.'+st).attr('src', count+'.png');
  Order.push(obj.id);
  Score.push(receipt_score[receipt_order.indexOf(obj.id)]);
  count += 1;
  //alert(Order);
});
/*
$('#').on('click', function(){
  var obj = event.target;
  var st = 'img_id_'+obj.id.toString();
  $('.'+st).attr('src', count+'.png');
  Order.push(obj.id);
  count += 1;
  alert(Order);
});
*/

$('.start_game').on('click', function(){
  if(count < 3){
    alert("select two or more players!!");
    return false;
  }
  if(0 > 0){
    if(count != (receipt_order.length+1)){
      alert("select all players");
      return false
    }
  }
  document.getElementById('Submit_score').value=Score.join(',');
  //alert(document.getElementById('Submit_score').value);
  //alert(document.getElementById('Submit_round').value);
  //alert('post:'+Order);
  document.getElementById('Order_id').value=Order;
/*
  var ele = document.createElement('input');
  ele.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');
  ele.setAttribute('name', 'order');
  ele.setAttribute('value', Order);
*/
});

</script>

<script>
var count = 1;
var Order = [];
var receipt_score = '0,0,0,0'.split(',');
var receipt_order = '1,2,3,4'.split(',');
var Score = [];
if(0 > 0){
  $('.contrl').hide();
}
$('.select').on('click', function(){
  var obj = event.target;
  obj.disabled = true;
  var st = 'img_id_'+obj.id.toString();
  $('.'+st).attr('src', count+'.png');
  Order.push(obj.id);
  Score.push(receipt_score[receipt_order.indexOf(obj.id)]);
  count += 1;
  //alert(Order);
});
/*
$('#').on('click', function(){
  var obj = event.target;
  var st = 'img_id_'+obj.id.toString();
  $('.'+st).attr('src', count+'.png');
  Order.push(obj.id);
  count += 1;
  alert(Order);
});
*/

$('.start_game').on('click', function(){
  if(count < 3){
    alert("select two or more players!!");
    return false;
  }
  if(0 > 0){
    if(count != (receipt_order.length+1)){
      alert("select all players");
      return false
    }
  }
  document.getElementById('Submit_score').value=Score.join(',');
  //alert(document.getElementById('Submit_score').value);
  //alert(document.getElementById('Submit_round').value);
  //alert('post:'+Order);
  document.getElementById('Order_id').value=Order;

  ele.setAttribute('value', Order);

});
